Generate me a questionnaire on Onboarding with 6 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Here is your requested Questionnaire:

 **What was the most memorable part of our company's new hire orientation process for this role (Select all that apply)?**
    - Meeting my supervisor/manager 
	- Reviewing job expectations and responsibilities  
   * Tour or overview facility/buildings   
  • Learning about benefits, policies & procedures
* Social event/network opportunity with colleagues

**How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our company's onboarding process for this role?**

• Excellent - I felt fully prepared to start my new position 
	- Good – The training was helpful but could be improved  
   * Fair/Neutral  (it met some, not all expectations)   
* Poor/Below Average    • It did little/nothing in preparing me 

**Were you provided with clear and concise job instructions/directions during the onboarding process?**

• Yes
	- No

How would rate your understanding of our company's policies & procedures after completing new hire orientation?

   * Excellent – I feel confident about knowing what to do 
    - Good  (I have a good idea, but could use some clarification)   
* Fair/Neutral     • It was okay/incomplete
	- Poor/Below Average      → Not clear at all

What suggestions or ideas would you like us consider for improving our company's onboarding process?

**Do any specific challenges did I face during my first few weeks in this role? If yes, please describe.**

Please feel free to provide additional feedback if there is anything else that comes up!
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Onboarding with 6 questions

[LLM ANSWER] -> JSON 
Here is the converted JSON:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "ONBOARDING",
        "NAME": "Onboarding Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "What was the most memorable part of our company's new hire orientation process for this role?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Meeting my supervisor/manager"},
              {"ANSWER": "Reviewing job expectations and responsibilities"},
              {"ANSWER": "Tour or overview facility/buildings"},
              {"ANSWER": "Learning about benefits, policies & procedures"},
              {"ANSWER": "Social event/network opportunity with colleagues"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our company's onboarding process for this role?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent - I felt fully prepared to start my new position"},
              {"ANSWER": "Good – The training was helpful but could be improved"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fair/Neutral  (it met some, not all expectations)"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor/Below Average    • It did little/nothing in preparing me"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "Were you provided with clear and concise job instructions/directions during the onboarding process?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "How would rate your understanding of our company's policies & procedures after completing new hire orientation?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent – I feel confident about knowing what to do"},
              {"ANSWER": "Good  (I have a good idea, but could use some clarification)"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fair/Neutral     • It was okay/incomplete"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor/Below Average      → Not clear at all"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "What suggestions or ideas would you like us consider for improving our company's onboarding process?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Please provide additional feedback if there is anything else that comes up!"},
              {"ANSWER": "Please describe any specific challenges you faced during your first few weeks in this role"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q6",
            "NAME": "Do any specific challenges did I face during my first few weeks in this role? If yes, please describe.",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Please provide additional feedback if there is anything else that comes up!"},
              {"ANSWER": "Please describe any specific challenges you faced during your first few weeks in this role"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

Note that I've used the `TYPE_ID` 2 for the first question, which is a multiple-choice question, and `TYPE_ID` 4 for the last two questions, which are open-ended feedback questions.
